<line act="0" scene="0" line="1" speaker="RUMOUR">Open your ears; for which of you will stop</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="2" speaker="RUMOUR">The vent of hearing when loud Rumour speaks?</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="3" speaker="RUMOUR">I, from the orient to the drooping west,</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="4" speaker="RUMOUR">Making the wind my post-horse, still unfold</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="5" speaker="RUMOUR">The acts commenced on this ball of earth:</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="6" speaker="RUMOUR">Upon my tongues continual slanders ride,</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="7" speaker="RUMOUR">The which in every language I pronounce,</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="8" speaker="RUMOUR">Stuffing the ears of men with false reports.</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="9" speaker="RUMOUR">I speak of peace, while covert enmity</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="10" speaker="RUMOUR">Under the smile of safety wounds the world:</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="11" speaker="RUMOUR">And who but Rumour, who but only I,</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="12" speaker="RUMOUR">Make fearful musters and prepared defence,</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="13" speaker="RUMOUR">Whiles the big year, swoln with some other grief,</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="14" speaker="RUMOUR">Is thought with child by the stern tyrant war,</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="15" speaker="RUMOUR">And no such matter? Rumour is a pipe</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="16" speaker="RUMOUR">Blown by surmises, jealousies, conjectures</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="17" speaker="RUMOUR">And of so easy and so plain a stop</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="18" speaker="RUMOUR">That the blunt monster with uncounted heads,</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="19" speaker="RUMOUR">The still-discordant wavering multitude,</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="20" speaker="RUMOUR">Can play upon it. But what need I thus</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="21" speaker="RUMOUR">My well-known body to anatomize</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="22" speaker="RUMOUR">Among my household? Why is Rumour here?</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="23" speaker="RUMOUR">I run before King Harry's victory;</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="24" speaker="RUMOUR">Who in a bloody field by Shrewsbury</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="25" speaker="RUMOUR">Hath beaten down young Hotspur and his troops,</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="26" speaker="RUMOUR">Quenching the flame of bold rebellion</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="27" speaker="RUMOUR">Even with the rebel's blood. But what mean I</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="28" speaker="RUMOUR">To speak so true at first? my office is</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="29" speaker="RUMOUR">To noise abroad that Harry Monmouth fell</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="30" speaker="RUMOUR">Under the wrath of noble Hotspur's sword,</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="31" speaker="RUMOUR">And that the king before the Douglas' rage</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="32" speaker="RUMOUR">Stoop'd his anointed head as low as death.</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="33" speaker="RUMOUR">This have I rumour'd through the peasant towns</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="34" speaker="RUMOUR">Between that royal field of Shrewsbury</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="35" speaker="RUMOUR">And this worm-eaten hold of ragged stone,</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="36" speaker="RUMOUR">Where Hotspur's father, old Northumberland,</line><line act="0" scene="0" line="37" speaker="RUMOUR">Lies crafty-sick: the posts speaker="LANCASTER">My fear is, your displeasure; my courtesy, my duty;</line><line act="5" scene="5" line="113" speaker="LANCASTER">and my speech, to beg your pardons. If you look</line><line act="5" scene="5" line="114" speaker="LANCASTER">for a good speech now, you undo me: for what I have</line><line act="5" scene="5" line="115" speaker="LANCASTER">to say is of mine own making; and what indeed I</line><line act="5" scene="5" line="116" speaker="LANCASTER">should say will, I doubt, prove mine own marring.</line><line act="5" scene="5" line="117" speaker="LANCASTER">But to the purpose, and so to the venture.
